Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1282, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 397. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 10. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 122

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 21 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 4 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 110 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 68

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 66 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Issue labelBadID

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 36

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_Label_RefValid, score 16 (for attribute does not reference a non-empty, unique id attribute of an input element)
  • Package wave, test a:label_orphaned, score 28 (Orphaned form label)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 35

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test link-name, score 3 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 24 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_1_1.H30.2, score 12 (img element is the only link content but has no text alternative)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 4 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 4 (Link has no text inside it)

Issue linkVague

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 32

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 73, score 30 (Link text is too generic to communicate the purpose or destination)

Issue linkTextsSame

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 30

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R9, score 7 (Links with identical accessible names have different purposes)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R44, score 7 (Links with identical accessible names and context serve different purposes)
  • Package tenon, test 98, score 22 (Links have the same text but different destinations)
